void FUNCNAME##\_reset(void) \

{ \

memset((void \*)&FUNCNAME##\_fake, 0, \

sizeof(FUNCNAME##\_fake) - sizeof(FUNCNAME##\_fake.custom\_fake) - \

sizeof(FUNCNAME##\_fake.custom\_fake\_seq)); \

FUNCNAME##\_fake.custom\_fake\_seq = NULL; \

FUNCNAME##\_fake.arg\_history\_len = [FFF\_ARG\_HISTORY\_LEN](#a7e08b23090c6385246513b05f4bcd948); \

}
